: qorwinebis Sewyveta, Svilis dabruneba alimentis


dakisreba.


aRwerilobiTi nawili:


2003w. 1 ivliss f. xaCiZem i. cxovrebaZis winaaRmdeg sarCeliT mi-


marTa xaSuris raionul sasamarTlos.


mosarCelem moiTxova qorwinebis Sewyveta Semdegi safuZvliT:


2000w. 21 martidan registrirebul qorwinebaSi imyofeba mopa-


suxesTan. erTad cxovrebis manZilze SeeZinaT ori Svili: T. _ da-


badebuli 1998 wels da s. _ dabadebuli 2000 wels. meuRlesTan


xSirad kamaTobda, bolo periodSi ki maTi erTad cxovreba SeuZ-


lebeli gaxda.


2003w. 14 marts i. cxovrebaZem Segebebuli sarCeliT mimarTa sasa-


marTlos. man moiTxova f. xaCiZisaTvis alimentis dakisreba da mamas-


Tan myofi T. xaCiZis aRsazrdelad gadacema.


xaSuris raionuli sasamarTlos 2003w. 4 seqtembris gadawyveti-


lebiT dakmayofilda f. xaCiZis sarCeli. Sewyda qorwineba f. xaCiZesa


da i. cxovrebaZes Soris.


aseve dakmayofilda i. cxovrebaZis Segebebuli sarCeli da 5 wlis


T. xaCiZe aRsazrdelad daubrunda dedas. f. xaCiZes alimentis saxiT


ori Svilis sazrdod daekisra 20 lari maT srulwlovnebamde.


Tbilisis saolqo sasamarTlos samoqalaqo, samewarmeo da gakot-


rebis saqmeTa palatis 2004w. 16 martis ganCinebiT f. xaCiZis saapela-


cio saCivari ar dakmayofilda da ucvlelad darCa mocemul saqmeze


raionuli sasamarTlos mier miRebuli gadawyvetileba.


saapelacio sasamarTlom miuTiTa sk-is 1202-e muxlze da aRniSna,


ganqorwinebis SemTxvevaSi, Tu visTan unda cxovrobdnen arasrul-


wlovani Svilebi damokidebulia mSoblebis SeTanxmebaze. SeuTan-


xmeblobis SemTxvevaSi davas gadawyvets sasamarTlos Svilebis inte-


resebis sasargeblod. mocemul SemTxvevaSi, vinaidan T. xaCiZe aris


mcirewlovani, misi movla-aRzrdisaTvis mizanSewonili iqneboda


2317


sacxovreblad dedasTan datoveba.


saapelacio sasamarTlom sk-is 1212-e da 1214-e muxlebis safuZ-


velze, rogorc alimentis dakisreba, ise misi odenoba kanonierad


miiCnia.


2004w. 1 ivniss f. xaCiZem sakasacio saCivriT mimarTa saqarTvelos


uzenaes sasamarTlos.


kasatorma moiTxova mocemul saqmeze miRebuli gadawyvetilebis


im nawilis gauqmeba, romliTac T. xaCiZe aRsazrdelad gadaeca dedas


da bavSvis aRsazrdelad masTan datoveba moiTxova im safuZvliT,


rom amJamad orive bavSvi masTan cxovrobs, amasTan dedas ar gaaCnia


aranairi Semosavali bavSvebis aRzrdisaTvis da bavSvebsac ar surT


dedasTan dabruneba.


kasators miaCnia, rom saapelacio sasamarTlom ar gamoiyena kano-


ni, romelic unda gamoeyenebina, kerZod, sk-is 1201-e muxli da aras-


worad ganmarta amave kodeqsis 1202-e muxli. 


samotivacio nawili:


sakasacio sasamarTlo sakasacio saCivris frglebSi gaecno saqmis


masalebs, moismina mxareTa ganmartebani da miaCnia, rom sakasacio sa-


Civari ar unda dakmayofildes Semdeg garemoebaTa gamo:


arasworia kasatoris miTiTeba imis Sesaxeb, rom TiTqos saapela-


cio sasamarTlom mocemuli davis gadawyvetis dros ar gamoiyena sk-


is 1201-e muxli.


miTiTebuli normis Tanaxmad, Tu ganqorwinebis an sxva mizezis ga-


mo mSoblebi cal-calke cxovrobdnen, maT SeTanxmebazea damokide-


buli, Tu visTan unda cxovrobdnen arasrulwlovani Svilebi. Seu-


Tanxmeblobis SemTxvevaSi davas gadawyvets sasamarTlo Svilebis in-


teresebis gaTvaliswinebiT.


saapelacio sasamarTlom, marTalia, Tavis ganCinebaSi ar miuTiTa


zemoT miTiTebuli normis numeracia, magram ganCinebis samotivacio


nawilSi miuTiTa, rom ganqorwinebis SemTxvevaSi, Tu visTan unda


cxovrobdnen arasrulwlovani Svilebi, damokidebulia mSobelTa


SeTanxmebaze. SeuTanxmeblobis SemTxvevaSi, davas gadawyvets sasa-


marTlo Svilebis interesebis gaTvaliswinebiT. swored amis safuZ-


velze gaakeTa saapelacio sasamarTlom daskvna, rom mocemul Sem-


TxvevaSi, imis gaTvaliswinebiT, rom T. xaCiZe iyo mcirewlovani, misi


movla-aRzrdisaTvis mizanSewonili iqneboda sacxovreblad dedas-


Tan datoveba.


aseve arasworia kasatoris miTiTeba imis Sesaxeb, rom TiTqos saa-


pelacio sasamarTlom arasworad ganmarta sk-is 1202-e muxli.


sakasacio sasamarTlo miuTiTebs, rom saapelacio sasamarTlos


sk-is 1202-e muxli ar ganumartavs. gadawyvetilebis samotivacio na-


wilSi, marTalia, saapelacio sasamarTlom moiyvana sk-is 1201-e mux-


2318


lis dispozicia da SecdomiT miuTiTa muxli #1202, magram es gare-


moeba ar warmoadgens 1202-e muxlis araswor ganmartebas. es aris me-


qanikuri Secdoma, romlis gasworebac SeuZlia sasamarTlos, ro-


gorc dainteresebuli mxaris, ise Tavisi iniciativiT, amasTan am Sec-


domiT ganCinebis Sinaarsi ar icvleba.


sakasacio sasamarTlo miuTiTebs, rom mSoblebis SeuTanxmeblo-


bis SemTxvevaSi Svilebis aRsazrdelad gadacemis sakiTxis gadaw-


yvetis dros sasamarTlo pirvel rigSi iTvaliswinebs Svilebis in-


teresebs. am interesebSi garda mSoblebis ekonomiuri mdgomareo-


bisa, gaTvaliswinebulia sxva garemoebebic, kerZod: kanoni ar


cnobs mamis raime upiratesobas Svilebis mimarT. arc dedas gaaCnia


aseTi ufleba. Svilebis aRsazrdelad gadacemis SemTxvevaSi ara


uflebaTa upiratesoba, aramed bavSvis sworad aRzrdis interese-


bia gadamwyveti. bavSvis aRzrdis interesebSi igulisxmeba ara mar-


to materialuri, aramed moraluri pirobebis Seqmna, amitom erT-


erT mSobels ar SeiZleba uari eTqvas, materialuri mdgomareobis


gamo, radgan es problema SeiZleba gamoswordes meore mSoblisTvis


alimentis dakisrebis gziT.


aRsaniSnavia is garemoeba, rom calke mcxovreb mSoblebs sasa-


marTlos mier sakiTxis gadawyvetis Semdeg ar erTmeva ufleba, rom


garkveuli drois gasvlis Semdeg xelaxla daayenos bavSvis gadace-


mis sakiTxi, Tu masTan bavSvis gazrdisaTvis saWiro aucilebeli pi-


robebi arsebobs da Tanac meore mSobeli saTanadod ar zrunavs


bavSvis aRzrdaze.


sk-is 1212-e muxlis Sesabamisad, mSoblebi movaleni arian arCinon


TavianTi arasrulwlovani Svilebi.


amave kodeqsis 1214-e muxlis Sesabamisad, Tu mSoblebi ver SeTan-


xmdebian alimentis odenobaze, maSin davas gadawyvets sasamarTlo.


alimentis odenobas sasamarTlo gadawyvets gonivruli, samarTlia-


ni Sefasebis safuZvelze Svilis normaluri rCena-aRzrdisaTvis au-


cilebeli moTxovnaTa farglebSi. alimentis odenobis gansazRvri-


sas sasamarTlo mxedvelobaSi iRebs, rogorc mSoblebis, ise Svilis


realur materialur mdgomareobas.


imis gaTvaliswinebiT, rom saqmeSi warmodgenili cnobis Sesabami-


sad, f. xaCiZis yovelTviuri xelfasi Seadgens 34 lars, sakasacio sa-


samarTlos miaCnia, rom rogorc alimentis odenoba, ise Svilis aR-

aRwerilobiTi nawili:


1998w. 21 maiss s.ipatovam sarCeliT mimarTa sasamarTlos z.beriZiS-


vilis winaaRmdeg da moiTxova anderZis baTilad cnoba. sarCelis sa-


fuZvlad mosarCelem aRniSna, rom q.TbilisSi, ... mdebare sacxovrebeli


saxlis 5/14 sakuTrebis uflebiT iricxeba masze, 2/14 z.beriZiSvilze,


xolo _ 7/14 aw gardacvlil z.piSnenkoze. z.piSnenko iyo misi deidaSvi-


li, igi gardaicvala 1995w. 22 aprils da mas sxva memkvidre mis garda ar


darCenia. samkvidro qoneba miiRo da daeufla z.piSnenkos gardacvale-


bisTanave. misTvis cnobili gaxda, rom samkvidro qonebaze pretenzias


acxadebs mopasuxe im safuZvliT, rom masze gacemulia Sinauruli an-


derZi, mosarCelis azriT, anderZi Sedgenilia kanonis moTxovnaTa uxe-


Si darRveviT. z.piSnenkos qonebaze memkvidreobis gaxsnis droisaTvis


Sinaurul anderZs moqmedi kanonmdebloba ar iTvaliswinebda.


mopasuxem sarCeli ar cno im safuZvliT, rom s.ipatova ar aris is

nawilSi misi moadgilis an morige eqimis mier. mocemul SemTxvevaSi ki

a.furcxvaniZem sarCeliT moiTxova saxlidan misi kuTvnili 1/2-is


realurad gamoyofa.


n. furcxvaniZem Segebebuli sarCeliT moiTxova misi kuTvnili


realuri wilis gazrda im motiviT, rom mas mosarCele


a.furcxvaniZem unda aunazRauros mis mier 1998-99 wlebSi saxlis


mSeneblobaze gaweuli xarjebi, aseve, dedisa da mamis dakrZalvis,


ormocisa da saflavis gakeTebaze gaweuli xarjebi. mama gardaicvala


1992 wels, xolo deda _ 1997 wels. n.furcxvaniZis mier gaweuli xarji


Seadgenda 58800 maneTis Sesabamis larsa da 2448 lars, romlis


gaTvaliswinebiTac unda gazrdiliyo misi kuTvnili wili


memkvidreobaSi.


wyaltubos raionulma sasamarTlom 2003w. 24 noembris


gadawyvetilebiT daakmayofila a.furcxvaniZis sarCeli,


n.furcxvaniZes ki Segebebul sarCelis dakmayofilebaze eTqva uari.


n.furcxvaniZem saapelacio saCivriT moiTxova wyaltubos


raionuli sasamarTlos gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba da misi Segebebuli


sarCelis dakmayofileba.


quTaisis saolqo sasamarTlosi apelantma daazusta saapelacio


saCivari da realuri wilis gazrdis nacvlad moiTxova


mopasuxisaTvis saziaro sagnis movla-Senaxvisa da mamkvidreblis


movla-patronobaze gaweuli xarjebis anazRaurebis dakisreba. misi


ganmartebiT, 75000 maneTi (anu 4500 lari) Seadgens mamis dakrZalvis


xarjebs. dedis dasaflavebaze da sxva ritualebze ki daixarja 2444


lari (sul oriveze 6948 lari), aseve apelantis mier saxlis


mSeneblobaze gaRebul iqna 25560 lari.


sul n. furcxvaniZem moiTxova 32508 laris anazRaureba.


saapelacio saCivris ganxilvisas apelantma n.furcxvaniZem da


misma warmomadgenelma m.doRonaZem daadastures saapelacio


saCivarSi gamoTqmuli mosazrebebi da moiTxoves wyaltubos


raionuli sasamarTlos gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba,

ritualebze gaweuli xarjebis saxiT 32508 laris gadaxdis dakisreba.

mkurnalobis, dakrZalvis, samkvidros dacvisa da marTvis, xelfasis

Semdeg garemoebaTa gamo:


sk-is 1507-e muxlis Tanaxmad, samoqalaqo kodeqsi vrceldeba


mxolod im urTierTobebze, romelic warmoiSoba am kodeqsis amo-


qmedebis Semdeg.


im urTierTobaTa mimarT, romlebic warmoiSoba sk-is ZalaSi


Sesvlamde, am kodeqsis normebi gamoiyeneba 1997w. 25 noembridan


warmoSobili uflebebis mimarT.


sk-is amoqmedebis gamo Zaladakarguli normatiuli aqtebis


safuZvelze warmoSobili urTierTobebis mimarT gamoiyeneba es nor-


matiuli aqtebi.


samoqalaqo samarTlis kodeqsis 544-e muxlis Tanaxmad, gar-


dacvlilis Svilebi kanoniT memkvidreobis dros memkvidreebad


iTvlebian Tanaswori wilis uflebiT.


Segebebuli sarCelis avtoris (kasatoris) moTxovna aris sacx-


ovrebeli saxlis mSeneblobis, mSoblebis dakrZalvasa da sxva rit-


ualebze gaweuli xarjebis anazRaureba.


udavoa, rom aRniSnuli faqtobrivi garemoebebi arsebobda sk-is amo-


qmedebamde da, Sesabamisad, maT safuZvelze warmoSobili davis gada-


sawyvetad gamoyenebul unda iqnes 1964w. samoqalaqo samarTlis kodeqsi.


samoqalaqo samarTlis kodeqsis me-80 muxlis Tanaxmad sasarCelo


xandazmulobis vada iwyeba sarCelis uflebis warmoSobis dRidan.


sarCelis ufleba warmoiSoba im dRes, rodesac pirma Seityo an unda


Seetyo Tavisi uflebis darRveva.

a.furcxvaniZe gardaicvala 1992 wels, b.furcxvaniZe _ 1997w. aprilSi.

kasatoris mier gaSvebul iqna sasarCelo xandazmulobis samwliani vada.

sanotaro organoSi an TviTmmarTvelobis adgilobriv organoSi


unda waredgina samkvidros gaxsnis dRidan eqvsi Tvis ganmavlobaSi.


am wesebis daucveloba iwvevs kuTvnili moTxovnis uflebis


dakargvas kreditorebis mier.

moqmedi saqarTvelos saqorwino da saojaxo kodeqsis me-80 muxlis


mixedviT, srulwlovani Svilebi movaleni arian, arCinon


Sromisuunaro mSoblebi, romlebsac daxmareba sWirdebaT.

qonebaze gaweuli gansakuTrebuli wvlilisaTvis, mas aRniSnuli pre-


tenziebi unda waeyenebina im samoqalaqo saqmeze, romliTac gadawyda

winaaRmdeg da moiTxova ojaxis wevrebTan erTad mopasuxis


gamosaxleba xaragaulis raionis sof. didvakeSi, pirvel sarTulze


mdebare rkinigzelTa oroTaxiani sacxovrebeli bina #9-dan Semdegi


safuZvlebiT:


mas, rogorc rkinigzis muSaks, xaragaulis raionis sof.


didvakeSi, rkinigzelTa bina #9-Si, pirvel sarTulze, aqvs


oroTaxiani sacxovrebeli bina. vinaidan igi meuRlesTan erTad,


ZiriTadad cxovrobda sof. marelisSi, 1994 wels dasaxelebuli bina


aTxova mopasuxes. meuRlis gardacvalebis gamo, mosarCelem ver


SeZlo sof.Si fizikuri Sroma da samsaxuri SeeTavsebina


erTmaneTisaTvis, ris gamoc mosTxova mopasuxes binis dacla,


romelzedac man uari ganucxada. mosarCelem misi moTxovnis


safuZvlad miuTiTa sk-is 172-e, 208-e, 218-e muxlebze.


Tavis werilobiT SesagebelSi mopasuxem ar cno sarCeli da


miuTiTa, rom mosarCeleze imave saxlSi me-2 sarTulze iricxeboda


sacxovrebeli bina, romelic man gayida 1988 wels, rac dadasturebu-


lia imavew. sasamarTlo gadawyvetilebiT. sadavo binaSi cxovrobda


givi maRraZe Tavisi ojaxiT 1988 wlamde. aRniSnulis Semdgom,


saqarTvelos rkinigzis #9 saxlmmarTvelobis administraciasTan


SeTanxmebiT, sadavo bina, rogorc rkinigzis sauwyebo bina, gamoeyo


sargeblobis uflebiT mopasuxes, sadac cxovrobs 1990 wlidan.


xaragaulis raionuli sasamarTlos 2002w. 1 ivlisis ganCinebiT,


mocemul saqmeSi mesame pirad damoukidebeli moTxovnis gareSe,


Cabmul iqna eleqtromomaragebis xaragaulis me-4 distancia.

gadawyvetilebiT vl. WolaZis sarCeli, dausabuTeblobisa da xan-


dazmulobis vadis gasvlis gamo, ar dakmayofilda, rac mosarCelem


saapelacio wesiT gaasaCivra.
